  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=8.2)
    The storytelling demonstrates sophisticated craft through vivid imagery and layered metaphors. The transformation of the character's stunt reel "converting explosions into kisses of light, falls into ascents" creates profound emotional resonance. The story successfully builds tension through the character's phobias and the mysterious echoes, resolving with a satisfying quietude. The theme of finding peace through confronting fears emerges organically, though occasionally the language becomes slightly overwrought. The subtext around identity and performance adds significant depth.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=8.7)

The recurring motifs of light/refraction and the transformation of promises into physical manifestations show sophisticated craft. The theme of reconciling human creativity with algorithmic power resonates beyond the immediate narrative, though some metaphors occasionally border on excessive.

The emotional arc moves from guilt to confrontation to acceptance without feeling rushed or sentimental. The ghosts' transformation from accusers to participants in healing demonstrates sophisticated narrative craft. The story rewards multiple readings with additional layers of meaning.
